					#Stasi Coup - Civil War if GER_stasi_var is at two but not three

					days = 10
					random_days = 25
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { 
						var = GER_stasi_var
						compare = less_than
						value = 2
					}
					#Stasi Coup - Nothing happens if the GER_stasi_var is less than 2
				}
				country_event = {
					id = rw_germany.100
					days = 10
					random_days = 24
				}
			}
		}

		}
	}

					set_variable = { GER_air_fuel = 0.04 }
				}
				force_update_dynamic_modifier = yes
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = GER_transport_fuel_effect
		}
	}
